---
about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> How does one construct\
  \ graphs that do not contain complete bipartite subgraphs of a given size? Professor\
  \ Zhao explains algebraic constructions known as norm graphs and more recent constructions\
  \ based on the use of random polynomials.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong>\
  \ Yufei Zhao</p>"
course_id: 18-217-graph-theory-and-additive-combinatorics-fall-2019

  <span m="287910">remind</span> <span m="288270">you,</span> <span m="290160">the</span>
  <span m="291170">norm</span> <span m="291570">map,</span> <span m="292410">if</span>
  <span m="292530">you</span> <span m="292650">have</span> <span m="292980">a</span>
  <span m="293040">field</span> <span m="293460">extension,</span> <span m="294590">in</span>
  <span m="294750">this</span> <span m="294930">case,</span> <span m="295200">specifically</span>
  <span m="295830">I</span> <span m="295910">am</span> <span m="295980">looking</span>
  <span m="296310">at</span> <span m="296460">the</span> <span m="296580">field</span>
  <span m="296940">extension,</span> <span m="299150">this</span> <span m="299610">Fp</span>
  <span m="300630">to</span> <span m="300780">the</span> <span m="300900">s,</span>
  <span m="302700">I</span> <span m="302790">can</span> <span m="302940">define</span>
  <span m="303480">a</span> <span m="303570">norm</span> <span m="303930">map</span>
  <span m="306270">as</span> <span m="306390">follows.</span> <span m="308700">Sending</span>
  <span m="309270">x</span> <span m="309960">to</span> <span m="310140">be</span>
  <span m="310710">the</span> <span m="310830">product</span> <span m="311850">of</span>
  <span m="313140">all</span> <span m="313380">the</span> <span m="314130">conjugates,</span>
  <span m="315060">or</span> <span m="315180">the</span> <span m="315270">Galois</span>
  <span m="315690">conjugates</span> <span m="316500">of</span> <span m="316680">x,</span>
  <span m="317820">in</span> <span m="317970">this</span> <span m="318180">field</span>
  <span m="318480">extension.</span> <span m="319740">So</span> <span m="319950">explicitly</span>
  <span m="320550">written</span> <span m="320730">out</span> <span m="321120">is</span>
  <span m="321300">just</span> <span m="321840">that</span> <span m="322050">expression,</span>
  <span m="323500">which</span> <span m="323910">I</span> <span m="324000">can</span>
  <span m="324600">clean</span> <span m="324960">and</span> <span m="325080">collect</span>

  <span m="326460">down</span> <span m="326820">like</span> <span m="327000">this.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="334650">the</span> <span m="334740">base</span> <span m="335040">field</span>
  <span m="335430">Fp.</span> <span m="336360">And</span> <span m="336570">that</span>
  <span m="336750">is</span> <span m="336870">because--</span> <span m="341388">well,</span>
  <span m="341880">one</span> <span m="342150">of</span> <span m="342210">the</span>
  <span m="342420">many</span> <span m="342690">reasons</span> <span m="343050">why</span>

  <span m="343620">case,</span> <span m="344280">is</span> <span m="344460">that</span>
  <span m="345060">if</span> <span m="345240">you</span> <span m="345390">look</span>
  <span m="345630">at--</span> <span m="347310">so</span> <span m="347670">I'll</span>

  <span m="653450">going</span> <span m="653590">to</span> <span m="653660">be</span>
  <span m="653750">something</span> <span m="654080">like</span> <span m="654260">that</span>
  <span m="654440">here.</span></p><p><span m="655550">So</span> <span m="655640">the</span>
  <span m="655730">claim</span> <span m="657530">is</span> <span m="657680">that</span>
  <span m="657830">this</span> <span m="658010">construction,</span> <span m="659420">this</span>
  <span m="659600">norm</span> <span m="659870">graph,</span> <span m="665410">is</span>

  <span m="2354560">random</span> <span m="2354890">graphs</span> <span m="2355220">case</span>

  <span m="2356660">but</span> <span m="2357650">it</span> <span m="2357740">will</span>
  <span m="2357890">have</span> <span m="2358130">some</span> <span m="2358400">new</span>
  <span m="2358610">ideas</span> <span m="2359300">coming</span> <span m="2359570">from</span>
  <span m="2359780">algebraic</span> <span m="2360230">geometry.</span></p><p><span
  m="2362820">First,</span> <span m="2363180">let's</span> <span m="2363390">show</span>
  <span m="2363690">that</span> <span m="2363990">this</span> <span m="2364170">graph</span>
  <span m="2364500">has</span> <span m="2365040">lots</span> <span m="2365430">of</span>
  <span m="2365610">edges.</span> <span m="2367360">And</span> <span m="2367380">that's</span>
  <span m="2368100">a</span> <span m="2368160">simple</span> <span m="2368550">calculation,</span>
  <span m="2370960">because</span> <span m="2372670">for</span> <span m="2373000">every</span>
  <span m="2373330">pair</span> <span m="2374530">of</span> <span m="2375160">points</span>
  <span m="2379360">of</span> <span m="2379560">vertices,</span> <span m="2381030">I</span>
  <span m="2381150">claim</span> <span m="2382620">that</span> <span m="2383650">the</span>
  <span m="2383850">probability--</span> <span m="2384620">so</span> <span m="2384780">here</span>
  <span m="2385110">f</span> <span m="2385350">is</span> <span m="2385500">the</span>
  <span m="2385590">random</span> <span m="2386040">object--</span> <span m="2386940">the</span>
  <span m="2387030">probability</span> <span m="2387690">that</span> <span m="2387870">f</span>
  <span m="2388380">evaluates</span> <span m="2389130">to</span> <span m="2389280">0</span>
  <span m="2389760">on</span> <span m="2389880">this</span> <span m="2390060">pair</span>
  <span m="2391190">is</span> <span m="2391920">exactly</span> <span m="2392640">q.</span>
  <span m="2393790">So</span> <span m="2393990">exactly</span> <span m="2394470">1</span>
  <span m="2394860">over</span> <span m="2395080">q,</span> <span m="2395810">1</span>
  <span m="2396000">over</span> <span m="2396210">the</span> <span m="2396330">size</span>
  <span m="2396660">of</span> <span m="2396750">the</span> <span m="2396810">field.</span>
  <span m="2398970">So</span> <span m="2398990">this</span> <span m="2399170">is</span>
  <span m="2399710">not</span> <span m="2399860">too</span> <span m="2399980">hard.</span></p><p><span
  m="2401930">And</span> <span m="2402050">the</span> <span m="2402140">reason</span>
  <span m="2402500">is</span> <span m="2402680">that</span> <span m="2403460">the</span>
  <span m="2403670">distribution</span> <span m="2404390">of</span> <span m="2404550">f</span>
  <span m="2406850">is</span> <span m="2410390">identical</span> <span m="2411360">to</span>
  <span m="2416150">if</span> <span m="2416330">you</span> <span m="2416750">are</span>
  <span m="2417260">an</span> <span m="2417440">extra</span> <span m="2417800">random</span>
  <span m="2418310">constant</span> <span m="2419120">on</span> <span m="2419300">f,</span>
  <span m="2432210">chosen</span> <span m="2432540">uniformly</span> <span m="2433170">at</span>
  <span m="2433290">random.</span> <span m="2434070">So</span> <span m="2434530">I</span>
  <span m="2434760">took</span> <span m="2434970">a</span> <span m="2435030">random</span>
  <span m="2435330">polynomial.</span> <span m="2435840">I</span> <span m="2435930">shifted</span>
  <span m="2436320">by</span> <span m="2436410">a</span> <span m="2436500">random</span>
  <span m="2436770">constant.</span> <span m="2437430">It's</span> <span m="2437550">still</span>
  <span m="2437820">uniformly</span> <span m="2438430">random</span> <span m="2438780">polynomial,</span>
  <span m="2439320">according</span> <span m="2439680">to</span> <span m="2439800">that</span>
  <span m="2439950">distribution.</span></p><p><span m="2441180">But</span> <span
  m="2441330">now,</span> <span m="2441810">you</span> <span m="2441930">see</span>
  <span m="2442500">that</span> <span m="2443220">this,</span> <span m="2445710">whatever</span>
  <span m="2446340">f</span> <span m="2446670">evaluated</span> <span m="2447290">to,</span>
  <span m="2447510">if</span> <span m="2447660">I</span> <span m="2447720">shift</span>
  <span m="2448110">by</span> <span m="2448320">a</span> <span m="2448380">random</span>
  <span m="2448860">constant,</span> <span m="2449810">you</span> <span m="2449940">will</span>
  <span m="2450090">end</span> <span m="2450270">up</span> <span m="2450420">with</span>
  <span m="2450540">a</span> <span m="2450600">uniform</span> <span m="2451020">distribution.</span>
  <span m="2453700">So</span> <span m="2453750">it</span> <span m="2453810">tells</span>
  <span m="2454080">you</span> <span m="2454650">that</span> <span m="2455820">that</span>
  <span m="2456000">guy</span> <span m="2456180">up</span> <span m="2456300">there</span>
  <span m="2456930">is</span> <span m="2458040">uniform</span> <span m="2458730">distribution</span>
  <span m="2463640">on</span> <span m="2463790">every</span> <span m="2465605">fixed</span>
  <span m="2468460">point</span> <span m="2469420">u,</span> <span m="2469540">v.</span>
  <span m="2471550">So</span> <span m="2471760">in</span> <span m="2471820">particular,</span>
  <span m="2472600">it</span> <span m="2472960">hits</span> <span m="2473260">0</span>
  <span m="2473620">with</span> <span m="2473800">probability</span> <span m="2474430">exactly</span>
  <span m="2474970">1</span> <span m="2475210">over</span> <span m="2475450">q.</span></p><p><span
  m="2478220">And</span> <span m="2478380">as</span> <span m="2478470">a</span> <span

  <span m="2480870">of</span> <span m="2481080">edges</span> <span m="2481920">of</span>
  <span m="2482040">g</span> <span m="2482730">in</span> <span m="2482880">the</span>
  <span m="2482940">expectation</span> <span m="2485310">is</span> <span m="2485640">exactly</span>
  <span m="2486630">n</span> <span m="2486790">squared</span> <span m="2488310">over</span>
  <span m="2488620">q,</span> <span m="2491410">where</span> <span m="2491620">n</span>
  <span m="2491980">is</span> <span m="2492160">the</span> <span m="2492250">number</span>
  <span m="2492550">of</span> <span m="2492610">vertices.</span> <span m="2494270">So</span>
  <span m="2494560">n</span> <span m="2494800">is</span> <span m="2496050">actually</span>
  <span m="2496450">not</span> <span m="2496670">the</span> <span m="2496690">number</span>
  <span m="2496940">of</span> <span m="2496980">vertices,</span> <span m="2497410">but</span>
  <span m="2497560">the</span> <span m="2498130">size</span> <span m="2498550">of</span>
  <span m="2498880">each</span> <span m="2499120">vertex</span> <span m="2499670">part,</span>
  <span m="2501010">namely</span> <span m="2501730">q</span> <span m="2501925">to</span>
  <span m="2502120">the</span> <span m="2502350">s.</span> <span m="2503655">So</span>
  <span m="2504090">you</span> <span m="2504190">see</span> <span m="2504290">that</span>
  <span m="2504450">it</span> <span m="2505680">gives</span> <span m="2506040">you</span>
  <span m="2506790">the</span> <span m="2506970">right</span> <span m="2507330">number</span>

  <span m="2508680">n</span> <span m="2508770">to</span> <span m="2508860">the</span>
  <span m="2508980">2</span> <span m="2509220">minus</span> <span m="2509580">1</span>
  <span m="2509760">over</span> <span m="2509970">s.</span> <span m="2511290">So</span>
  <span m="2511410">we</span> <span m="2511530">have</span> <span m="2511740">the</span>
  <span m="2511830">right</span> <span m="2512100">number</span> <span m="2512340">of</span>
  <span m="2512460">edges.</span></p><p><span m="2513280">And</span> <span m="2513330">now,</span>
  <span m="2513660">we</span> <span m="2513840">want</span> <span m="2514080">to</span>
  <span m="2514950">show</span> <span m="2515520">that</span> <span m="2516690">this</span>

  <span m="2521780">might</span> <span m="2521970">have</span> <span m="2522240">some</span>
  <span m="2522450">copies</span> <span m="2522870">of</span> <span m="2522990">Kst's.</span>

  <span m="2524160">unavoidable.</span> <span m="2525620">Just</span> <span m="2526100">as</span>

  <span m="2527970">have</span> <span m="2528180">some</span> <span m="2528360">copies</span>
  <span m="2528750">of</span> <span m="2528840">Kst's.</span> <span m="2529650">But</span>
  <span m="2529830">if</span> <span m="2529950">they</span> <span m="2530070">are</span>
  <span m="2530130">not</span> <span m="2530370">too</span> <span m="2530640">many</span>
  <span m="2530880">copies,</span> <span m="2531360">I</span> <span m="2531450">can</span>
  <span m="2531690">remove</span> <span m="2532050">them</span> <span m="2532590">and</span>
  <span m="2532740">obtain</span> <span m="2533160">a</span> <span m="2533220">Kst</span>
  <span m="2533760">free</span> <span m="2533970">graph.</span></p><p><span m="2537830">OK,</span>
  <span m="2538930">so</span> <span m="2539050">what</span> <span m="2539220">is</span>

  <span m="2542200">when</span> <span m="2542590">you</span> <span m="2542770">have</span>
  <span m="2543280">a</span> <span m="2543400">genuine</span> <span m="2544150">Erdos-Renyi</span>
  <span m="2544860">random</span> <span m="2545170">graph?</span> <span m="2547260">Well,</span>
  <span m="2547800">what</span> <span m="2548040">is</span> <span m="2548190">the</span>
  <span m="2548340">expected</span> <span m="2549360">number</span> <span m="2549900">of</span>

  <span m="2556350">if</span> <span m="2556530">you</span> <span m="2557820">fix</span>
  <span m="2559050">some</span> <span m="2559320">u</span> <span m="2561150">with</span>

  <span m="2566960">vertices,</span> <span m="2569600">I</span> <span m="2569690">want</span>
  <span m="2569870">to</span> <span m="2569960">understand,</span> <span m="2570800">how</span>
  <span m="2571010">many</span> <span m="2572420">common</span> <span m="2572750">neighbors</span>
  <span m="2581610">does</span> <span m="2581860">u</span> <span m="2582040">have?</span>
  <span m="2590000">But</span> <span m="2590230">because</span> <span m="2590530">the</span>
  <span m="2590590">common</span> <span m="2590890">neighbors,</span> <span m="2591220">if</span>
  <span m="2591340">he</span> <span m="2591430">has</span> <span m="2591700">too</span>
  <span m="2591880">many</span> <span m="2592090">common</span> <span m="2592390">neighbors,</span>
  <span m="2593170">then</span> <span m="2593380">that's</span> <span m="2593650">a</span>
  <span m="2593710">Kst.</span></p><p><span m="2596820">It</span> <span m="2596950">is</span>
  <span m="2597070">not</span> <span m="2597340">hard</span> <span m="2598150">to</span>
  <span m="2598210">calculate</span> <span m="2598780">the</span> <span m="2598960">expectation</span>
  <span m="2600070">of</span> <span m="2600220">this</span> <span m="2600400">quantity,</span>
  <span m="2601120">both</span> <span m="2601480">in</span> <span m="2601630">the</span>

  <span m="2604780">And</span> <span m="2604870">you</span> <span m="2604930">can</span>

  <span m="2609160">expected</span> <span m="2609790">number</span> <span m="2611140">of</span>
  <span m="2611320">common</span> <span m="2611650">neighbors</span> <span m="2612570">is</span>
  <span m="2613330">exactly</span> <span m="2614560">n</span> <span m="2615220">to</span>

  <span m="2617140">the</span> <span m="2617230">minus</span> <span m="2618290">s.</span>
  <span m="2619210">So</span> <span m="2619470">there</span> <span m="2619750">are</span>
  <span m="2619990">s</span> <span m="2620230">elements</span> <span m="2620620">of</span>
  <span m="2620800">u,</span> <span m="2621610">which</span> <span m="2621820">is</span>
  <span m="2621940">exactly</span> <span m="2622510">1.</span> <span m="2625980">And</span>
  <span m="2626100">you</span> <span m="2626220">know</span> <span m="2626430">that</span>
  <span m="2626700">for</span> <span m="2626910">a</span> <span m="2627000">binomial</span>

  <span m="2629820">1</span> <span m="2630600">and</span> <span m="2630740">a</span>
  <span m="2630780">large</span> <span m="2631170">number</span> <span m="2631500">of</span>
  <span m="2631710">variables,</span> <span m="2632910">the</span> <span m="2633090">distribution</span>
  <span m="2633720">is</span> <span m="2633810">approximately</span> <span m="2634500">Poissonian.</span></p><p><span
  m="2643802">Ah,</span> <span m="2644290">but</span> <span m="2644470">that's</span>
  <span m="2644650">in</span> <span m="2644740">the</span> <span m="2644830">case</span>
  <span m="2645130">when</span> <span m="2645340">it's</span> <span m="2646630">independently</span>
  <span m="2647290">distributed,</span> <span m="2651640">which</span> <span m="2651840">is</span>
  <span m="2652030">the</span> <span m="2652120">case</span> <span m="2652450">in</span>

  <span m="2653000">GMP.</span> <span m="2654760">But</span> <span m="2654940">it</span>
  <span m="2655000">turns</span> <span m="2655300">out</span> <span m="2655960">for</span>
  <span m="2656560">the</span> <span m="2656710">algebraic</span> <span m="2657370">setting</span>
  <span m="2657760">we're</span> <span m="2657940">doing</span> <span m="2658240">here,</span>
  <span m="2659080">things</span> <span m="2659620">don't</span> <span m="2659890">behave</span>
  <span m="2660490">independently.</span> <span m="2662240">It's</span> <span m="2662290">not</span>
  <span m="2662500">that</span> <span m="2662590">you're</span> <span m="2662740">doing</span>
  <span m="2662950">coin</span> <span m="2663280">flops</span> <span m="2663670">for</span>
  <span m="2663820">every</span> <span m="2665450">possible</span> <span m="2665900">edge.</span>
  <span m="2666170">We're</span> <span m="2666320">doing</span> <span m="2666590">some</span>
  <span m="2666830">randomized</span> <span m="2667490">algebraic</span> <span m="2667940">construction.</span></p><p><span
  m="2668800">And</span> <span m="2669020">for</span> <span m="2669230">algebraic</span>
  <span m="2669710">geometry</span> <span m="2670250">reasons,</span> <span m="2671110">you</span>
  <span m="2671240">will</span> <span m="2671360">see</span> <span m="2671570">that</span>
  <span m="2671960">the</span> <span m="2672110">distribution</span> <span m="2672650">is</span>
  <span m="2672800">very</span> <span m="2673040">much</span> <span m="2673280">not</span>
  <span m="2673670">like</span> <span m="2673920">Poissonian.</span> <span m="2675660">It</span>
  <span m="2675750">will</span> <span m="2675840">turn</span> <span m="2676110">out</span>
  <span m="2676560">that</span> <span m="2676800">either</span> <span m="2678500">the</span>
  <span m="2678570">number</span> <span m="2678840">of</span> <span m="2678930">common</span>
  <span m="2679260">neighbors</span> <span m="2680040">is</span> <span m="2680850">bounded</span>
  <span m="2682110">or</span> <span m="2682710">it</span> <span m="2682830">is</span>
  <span m="2682980">very</span> <span m="2683250">large.</span> <span m="2686810">And</span>
  <span m="2687950">that</span> <span m="2688130">means</span> <span m="2688760">that</span>
  <span m="2688910">we</span> <span m="2689120">can</span> <span m="2690410">show</span>
  <span m="2690940">using</span> <span m="2691760">some</span> <span m="2692150">Markov</span>
  <span m="2692550">inequality</span> <span m="2693620">that</span> <span m="2693920">the</span>
  <span m="2694010">probability</span> <span m="2694610">that</span> <span m="2694760">it</span>
  <span m="2694850">is</span> <span m="2694970">very</span> <span m="2695270">large</span>
  <span m="2695960">is</span> <span m="2696080">quite</span> <span m="2696380">small.</span>
  <span m="2697130">So</span> <span m="2697250">typically,</span> <span m="2697820">it</span>
  <span m="2697940">will</span> <span m="2698060">not</span> <span m="2698360">have</span>
  <span m="2698630">many</span> <span m="2699290">common</span> <span m="2699710">neighbors?</span>
  <span m="2702300">And</span> <span m="2702440">that's</span> <span m="2702650">the</span>
  <span m="2702740">intuition,</span> <span m="2703530">and</span> <span m="2703760">so</span>
  <span m="2704180">let's</span> <span m="2704600">work</span> <span m="2704810">out</span>
  <span m="2704940">this</span> <span m="2705110">intuition.</span> <span m="2706740">Any</span>
  <span m="2706970">questions</span> <span m="2707300">so</span> <span m="2707450">far?</span></p><p><span
  m="2712220">So</span> <span m="2712380">how</span> <span m="2712500">do</span> <span
  m="2712590">we</span> <span m="2712680">do</span> <span m="2712830">this</span>

  <span m="3046430">random</span> <span m="3046750">indeterminate</span> <span m="3047940">is</span>
  <span m="3048220">invertible.</span></p><p><span m="3051240">Here,</span> <span

  <span m="3054250">So</span> <span m="3055470">let's</span> <span m="3055650">do</span>
  <span m="3055890">Lagrange</span> <span m="3056320">interpolation</span> <span m="3056940">twice,</span>
  <span m="3057900">once</span> <span m="3058290">for</span> <span m="3058740">each</span>
  <span m="3059010">variable.</span> <span m="3061920">So</span> <span m="3061970">we'll</span>
  <span m="3062180">apply</span> <span m="3067930">Lagrange</span> <span m="3068950">interpolation</span>
  <span m="3073616">twice.</span> <span m="3076030">So</span> <span m="3076190">the</span>
  <span m="3076280">first</span> <span m="3076580">time,</span> <span m="3077450">we'll</span>
  <span m="3077600">see</span> <span m="3077870">that</span> <span m="3078080">for</span>
  <span m="3078320">all</span> <span m="3080620">values</span> <span m="3081750">of</span>
  <span m="3081970">u,</span> <span m="3083360">there</span> <span m="3083510">exists</span>
  <span m="3084920">a</span> <span m="3085970">single</span> <span m="3086450">variate</span>
